id="tab_7_28AE3B_head" data-nc="" data-nr="" class="b_dmtab" style=" width:100px;" data-w="100" data-ow="132" data-content="tab_7_28AE3B" role="tab" aria-controls="tab_7_28AE3B" aria-selected="false" class="tab-content"><div id="tab_1_28A5EF" data-appns="SERP" data-k="5549.2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab_1_28A5EF_head" data-priority=""><div class="b_clearfix b_overflow"><div class="b_floatR_img"><div class="cico" style="width:100px;height:100px;"><img height="100" width="100" data-src-hq="https://th.bing.com/th?id=ODL.6947628f777878a6e48bc3f635122313&amp;w=100&amp;h=100&amp;c=12&amp;pcl=faf9f7&amp;o=6&amp;pid=13.1" role="presentation" data-priority="2" id="emb16C7E258E" class="rms_img" src="https://th.bing.com/th?id=ODL.6947628f777878a6e48bc3f635122313&amp;w=100&amp;h=100&amp;c=12&amp;pcl=faf9f7&amp;o=6&amp;pid=13.1" data-bm="56"></div></div><p class="b_paractl">The speed of light in <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=d93c191a8be2333cJmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU1OA&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPVZhY3V1bSUyMHdpa2lwZWRpYSZmb3JtPVdJS0lSRQ&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5558.1">vacuum</a>, commonly denoted c, is a universal <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=89a1a154374bbdbcJmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU1OQ&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPVBoeXNpY2FsJTIwY29uc3RhbnQlMjB3aWtpcGVkaWEmZm9ybT1XSUtJUkU&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5559.1">physical constant</a> that is exactly equal to 299,792,458 metres per second (approximately 300,000 kilometres per second; 186,000 miles per second; 671 million miles per hour).  According to the <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=4b37a32b28ab84d3JmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU2MA&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPVNwZWNpYWwlMjByZWxhdGl2aXR5JTIwd2lraXBlZGlhJmZvcm09V0lLSVJF&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5560.1">special theory of relativity</a>, c is the upper limit for the speed at which conventional <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=88e6aba022c65b8fJmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU2MQ&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPU1hdHRlciUyMHdpa2lwZWRpYSZmb3JtPVdJS0lSRQ&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5561.1">matter</a> or <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=0dcb12571151eff8JmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU2Mg&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPUVuZXJneSUyMHdpa2lwZWRpYSZmb3JtPVdJS0lSRQ&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5562.1">energy</a> (and thus any <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=2a286c5e2f1c2193JmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU2Mw&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPVNpZ25hbCUyMHdpa2lwZWRpYSZmb3JtPVdJS0lSRQ&amp;ntb=1" h="ID=SERP,5563.1">signal</a> carrying <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bing.com/ck/a?!&amp;&amp;p=05651ab9ba7f22e6JmltdHM9MTY5OTE0MjQwMCZpZ3VpZD0zMTVjNTA2Ni04NWJjLTYwMTItMjA5NC00M2E2ODRhYzYxYTYmaW5zaWQ9NTU2NA&amp;ptn=3&amp;hsh=3&amp;fclid=315c5066-85bc-6012-2094-43a684ac61a6&amp;u=a1L3NlYXJjaD9xPUluZm9ybWF0aW9uJTIwd2lraXBlZGlhJmZvcm09V0lLSVJF&amp;ntb=1"
